<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">
<P STYLE="margin: 0; text-align: right"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, 
Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 8pt"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin: 0; text-align: right">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin: 0; text-align: right"></P>
<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"></P>
<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"></P>
<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>Energy Fuels 
Announces High-Grade Uranium Intercepts at Nichols
Ranch ISR Project</B></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 9.75pt 0">LAKEWOOD, 
CO, Aug. 15, 2016 /CNW/ - <B>Energy Fuels Inc. (NYSE
MKT: UUUU; TSX: EFR) (&quot;Energy Fuels&quot; or the &quot;Company&quot;)</B>, 
a leading producer of uranium in the United States,
is pleased to announce that it has intercepted several large and high-grade 
areas of mineralization in the next wellfield expected
to go into production at its Nichols Ranch ISR Project (&quot;Nichols 
Ranch&quot;) in Wyoming, USA.&nbsp; On August 1, 2016, the
Company began delineation drilling and the installation of the wellfield to be 
associated with Header House 9 at Nichols Ranch.
&nbsp;Currently, four rigs are being utilized to drill pilot holes, ream, case, 
and complete the injection and recovery wells for
this wellfield. &nbsp;Header House 9 is expected to begin producing uranium 
later in 2016.&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 9.75pt 0">To date, a 
total of 52 holes in this new wellfield have been
drilled.&nbsp; Of the 52 holes, 46 have encountered mineralization which is 
above the grade % x thickness (&quot;GT&quot;) cut-off
of 0.3.&nbsp; This includes one hole which encountered 5.0 feet of 
mineralization with an average grade of 2.40% eU<SUB>3</SUB>O<SUB>8</SUB>.&nbsp;
In addition, many of the holes have encountered multiple intercepts above the GT
cutoff.&nbsp; It is anticipated that a total of
120 wells will be incorporated into Header House 9.&nbsp; The table below 
contains data for the 10 best holes drilled to date in
this wellfield:</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; border: black 1pt 
solid; font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: bottom">

    <TD COLSPAN="4" STYLE="padding: 1.5pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, 
Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 8pt">* GT represents grade multiplied by the 
thickness and is calculated by multiplying eU3O8 grade (in percent) by gamma 
anomaly thickness (in feet) as determined from down-hole radiometric probing. 
For example, a drill hole that has 10 feet of 0.10% uranium mineralization has a
GT of 1.0 and would be considered a good hole by ISR mining 
standards.</FONT></TD></TR>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 9.75pt 0">Stephen P. 
Antony, President and CEO of Energy Fuels stated:&nbsp;
&quot;The drill results we are seeing in the wellfield for Header House 9 at 
Nichols Ranch are very positive, and the uranium grades
and thicknesses are significantly exceeding expectations.&nbsp; Indeed, it is 
quite rare to encounter mineralization in U.S. ISR
projects that have grades above 2.0% U<SUB>3</SUB>O<SUB>8</SUB> and GT values 
above 10.&nbsp; Due to the size of the wellfield,
expected number of wells, and the quality of mineralization we are encountering,
we expect this to be the largest and most productive
portion of the wellfield at Nichols Ranch to date.&nbsp; Overall, the Nichols 
Ranch deposit continues to deliver results that exceed
our original expectations.&nbsp; We look forward to producing uranium from this 
new wellfield beginning later this year.&quot;</P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 9.75pt 0"><B><I>About
Energy Fuels:&nbsp; </I></B><I>Energy Fuels is
a leading integrated US-based uranium mining company, supplying 
U<SUB>3</SUB>O<SUB>8</SUB> to major nuclear utilities.&nbsp; Energy
Fuels holds three of America's key uranium production centers, the White Mesa 
Mill in Utah, the Nichols Ranch Processing Facility
in Wyoming, and the Alta Mesa Project in Texas.&nbsp; The White Mesa Mill is the
only conventional uranium mill operating in the
U.S. today and has a licensed capacity of over 8 million pounds of 
U<SUB>3</SUB>O<SUB>8</SUB> per year.&nbsp; The Nichols Ranch
Processing Facility is an ISR production center with a licensed capacity of 2 
million pounds of U<SUB>3</SUB>O<SUB>8</SUB> per
year.&nbsp; Alta Mesa is an ISR production center currently on care and 
maintenance.&nbsp; Energy Fuels also has the largest NI
43-101 compliant uranium resource portfolio in the U.S. among producers, and 
uranium mining projects located in a number of Western
U.S. states, including one producing ISR project, mines on standby, and mineral 
properties in various stages of permitting and
development.&nbsp; The Company's common shares are listed on the NYSE MKT under 
the trading symbol &quot;UUUU&quot;, and on the
Toronto Stock Exchange under the trading symbol &quot;EFR&quot;.</I></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 9.75pt 
0"><B><I>Stephen P. Antony, P.E., President &amp; CEO of Energy
Fuels</I></B><I>, is a Qualified Person as defined by Canadian National 
Instrument 43-101 and has reviewed and approved the technical
disclosure contained in this news release. &nbsp;</I></P>
